    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer3018146224734325034">The Art of Startup Fundraising takes a fresh look at raising money for startups, with a focus on the changing face of startup finance. New regulations are making the old go-to advice less relevant, as startup money is increasingly moving online. These new waters are all but uncharted—and founders need an accessible guide. This book helps you navigate the online world of st</span>
  <span id="freeText3018146224734325034" style="display:none">The Art of Startup Fundraising takes a fresh look at raising money for startups, with a focus on the changing face of startup finance. New regulations are making the old go-to advice less relevant, as startup money is increasingly moving online. These new waters are all but uncharted—and founders need an accessible guide. This book helps you navigate the online world of startup fundraising with easy-to-follow explanations and expert perspective on the new digital world of finance. You'll find tips and tricks on raising money and investing in startups from early stage to growth stage, and develop a clear strategy based on the new realities surrounding today's startup landscape.<br /><br />The finance world is in a massive state of flux. Changes are occurring at an increasing pace in all sectors, but few more intensely than the startup sphere. When the paradigm changes, your processes must change with it. This book shows you how startup funding works, with expert coaching toward the new rules on the field.<br /><br />-Learn how the JOBS Act impacts the fundraising model<br />-Gain insight on startups from early stage to growth stage<br />-Find the money you need to get your venture going<br />-Craft your pitch and optimize the strategy<br />-Build momentum<br />-Identify the right investors<br />-Avoid the common mistakes<br /><br />Don't rely on the "how we did it" tales from superstar startups, as these stories are unique and applied to exceptional scenarios. The game has changed, and playing by the old rules only gets you left behind. Whether you're founding a startup or looking to invest, The Art of Startup Fundraising provides the up-to-the-minute guidance you need.<br /><br />PRAISE FOR THE ART OF STARTUP FUNDRAISING:<br /><br />“The Art of Startup Fundraising is a must read for anyone who even considers starting a business. Fundraising is hard. This book gives you the roadmap to get where you are going. Alejandro Cremades speaks with wisdom and from experience.“ <br /><br />- Tim Draper , Founder of Draper Associates, DFJ, and Draper University.<br /><br />"The Art of Startup Fundraising should be a mandatory reading for entrepreneurs that are looking to raise capital. This book will enable Alejandro to help many more early stage companies answer the tough questions when fundraising." <br /><br />- Marco Landi, Former Chief Operating Officer at Apple and Chairman at Atlantis Ventures<br /><br />"Raising capital is often the most daunting and least understood aspects of starting a new business and there are few people more experienced than Alejandro Cremades to act as a guide. The Art of Startup Fundraising unlocks key secrets of fundraising for newly minted entrepreneurs." <br /><br />- Jeff Stibel, Chairman of BrainGate, Inc. and Vice Chairman of Dun &amp; Bradstreet, Inc.; New York Times bestselling author of Breakpoint and Wired for Thought.<br /><br />"This book provides a clear, concise tour of the fundraising game. With his crowdfunding and entrepreneurial expertise in full display, Cremades does a terrific job making a complicated process simple and accessible." <br /><br />- Jeff Bussgang, General Partner at Flybridge Capital Partners and Senior Lecturer at Harvard Business School<br /><br />“Entrepreneurs need to be amazing at recruiting, selling and fundraising. The Art of Startup Fundraising provides the essential toolkit for mastering a core skill for any entrepreneur.” <br /><br />- Gil Penchina, serial entrepreneur and prolific angel investor<br /><br />“For many entrepreneurs finding the right investor for their venture can be a daunting task. Alejandro's experience with equity crowdfunding gives a unique perspective on the fundraising game. The Art of Startup Fundraising is very insightful for entrepreneurs looking to close a round of financing and changing the world.” <br /><br />- Anyndya Ghose, Professor at NYU Stern School of Business<br /><br />“There is no perfect approach to raising investment for a startup, but there is a certain tribal knowledge out there, that most of us had to learn through several failed attempts. The Art of Startup Fundraising captures every bit of advice (and then some!) that I would give to any entrepreneur looking for funding.” <br /><br />- Paul Murphy, Partner at Betaworks and CoFounder of Playdots<br /><br />“Alejandro's The Art of Startup Fundraising is a must read for any entrepreneur. Clear and concise, he outlines in today's startup community the steps to successfully fundraise. This is the golden era for entrepreneurs, any good idea with proof of concept can get access to money. Know your options!” <br /><br />- Angelo J. Robles, Founder and CEO of Family Office Association<br /><br />“It doesn't matter how great of a business you can build. If you can't raise money, you're toast. Master this book.” <br /><br />- Ilya Pozin, Forbes Contributor and CoFounder of Pluto TV and CoFounder of Coplex<br /><br />"The Art of Startup Fundraising translates art into science. By sharing proven formulas, strategies, and case studies that work, Alejandro Cremades provides a needed service to future entrepreneurs." <br /><br />- Josh Cohen, Managing Partner at City Light Capital<br /><br />“This ought to be a reading requirement for all entrepreneurs when building a business and raising capital. This is a very well written and informative book, written by a man who is a testament to dedication and creativity when confronted with the challenges of being an entrepreneur and raising capital.” <br /><br />- Carter Caldwell, serial entrepreneur and Principal at Cross Atlantic Capital Partners<br /><br />“Alejandro is on the bleeding edge of equity crowdfunding today. When he talks about fundraising, startups listen.” <br /><br />- Andrew Ackerman, Managing Director at Dreamit Ventures<br /><br />“Raising capital can be tough. Alejandro provides a step-by-step guidebook to all entrepreneurs that rather spend their time thinking about changing the world instead of thinking of how to raise funds.” <br /><br />- Tobias P. Schirmer, Managing Partner of JOIN Capital <br /><br />"A superb book on fundraising. Alejandro's guidance should arm entrepreneurs with the necessary tools to close with success a meaningful round of financing." <br /><br />- Ellen Weber, Executive Director at Robin Hood Ventures<br /><br />“The Art of Startup Fundraising is a practical and comprehensive resource for entrepreneurs to use again and again. It captures what startups need to do to be successful in the rapidly evolving financing world, while also providing tips on the fundamentals of building businesses that don’t change over time.” <br /><br />- Marianne Hudson, Executive Director at Angel Capital Association<br /><br />“Raising money is hard. But start-up founders all over the world can make it exponentially easier by educating themselves on the process of raising equity capital before they dive into it. The practical, hands-on advice from Alejandro Cremades in this book provides a solid foundation in that self-education process. Delivered in an approachable format with a key lesson to take-away every few pages, “The Art of Startup Fundraising” is essential reading for entrepreneurs everywhere.” <br /><br />- Allen Taylor, Managing Director at Endeavor</span>

I couldn't recommend this book any more highly for those with a desire to quickly learn the ins and outs of raising start-up capital.   <span id="freeText13614532712786016300" style="display:none">This book is a rare glimpse into the mind of a true industry insider with practical data and modern business understanding applicable to any would-be inventor or business person. I couldn't recommend this book any more highly for those with a desire to quickly learn the ins and outs of raising start-up capital. Covering everything from crowd funding online to schmoozing investors in person, Alejandro Cremades describes the skills required of a contemporary entrepreneur. <br /> Informative, sophisticated and inspiring The Art of Startup Fundraising is a comprehensive guide for any entrepreneur in the twenty-first century. Carrying the reader through the steps of funding a new idea, Alejandro Cremades debunks popularized archetypes of venture capitalism with his sobering analysis of fundraising in varying economic environments. <br /> Nestled between the genre's of “how to” and “economics” Cremades gives us a fact based outline of generating the initial capital for any new business or product. True to the tenets of economics while still regarding the very real modern phenomena of speculative markets The Art of Startup Fundraising provides sound milestones and realistic expectations as well as the techniques to achieve your goals. </span>

                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1796721106&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1796721106" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16020987324366774007">a lot of practical advices and insights into investors-startups relationship and the related decision making and the workflow. <span id="freeTextContainer7336096183282740905">Of course this is nonfiction book. I think everyone will love it. The book was very well written. I did not find a single flowery sentence nor wordy.   <span id="freeText7336096183282740905" style="display:none">Of course this is nonfiction book. I think everyone will love it. The book was very well written. I did not find a single flowery sentence nor wordy. Even all sentences is not "too business". That makes this book could be categorized as an easy reading one, well..at least that was what i thought. Even you can comfortably read it in the backyard with a cup of tea and listen to the music. Without having intended for intensive reading, you can easily understand the contents of this book and benefit from it. <br />I recommend this for everyone. You do not have to be a businessman or who intend to do business. But of course this book would be more helpful for those who intend to start a business and ones who want to promote their existing businesses. In this book the author delivered his ideas based on his personal's experience as a superior businessman. He also gave applicable examples how to act or do in some situations with certain purpose. Step by step to reach the break even point then profit. You can also read how he founded Onevest, a company that helps entrepreneurs funding capital. When he and his wife started all that from her apartment and a year later his platform was written in TIME as one of the best crowdfunding platforms in the word!<br />The author does not even forget to touch the psychological side of an entrepreneur. How to manage emotion in certain conditions. <br />My favorite part is when the authors describe how he size up a person as a true entrepreneur. The ones must have a street smart, and are also a risk taker. Getting to know more the personal life of the author. I think this is interesting because he himself is so inspiring, vibrant, full of vision and open minded.<br />All stars for this book.<br /> <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText15273847717157956367" style="display:none">Some of the greatest ideas never see the light of the day because either there is no immediate scope for them and/or they don’t have enough capital to get the ball rolling. This book will bridge this gap and will help readers in adapting their ideas to make them profitable. <br />World has never seen the power of start-ups as much as it witnesses today. Start-ups with advent of crowd-funding and venture capitalists have become a major stimulus to economies around the globe. This book addresses all the ambiguities and clarifies them in a walk-through for anyone to convert a great idea into a successful enterprise. It compiles, and more importantly rectifies the conceptual fallacies that are normally not found in books and (may be) are scattered over internet. The new millennium economies are fostering SMEs across the globe- and this is a DIY handbook, for every entrepreneur to succeed without losing the trade-secrets. It will serve the readers as a consultant, confidante and big brother you need to lean on. It all starts with generating capital and connecting it with revenue- and this book is a tell-all tale. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText8407493302203301901" style="display:none">Capital and revenue is what makes businesses tick. It gives a sense purpose- whether its goods, services, idea, place or person. It also gives credibility and respect to all those involve. You may be a novice, newbie or even a seasoned entrepreneur- looking to promote and project your ideas towards profitability. This read will serve you as a point of reference, a go-to guide and just a quick chronology- of how to approach investors to fuel your new business promptly. It provides you all- from class room text knowledge to street smart strategies- that will work to your advantage and also in the investor’s favor. It gives you a glimpse of investor’s mindset with what to say and (wisely) what not to say in a given situation. It further polishes your art of negotiation and to make the best for yourself and thereby your business. It’s not a book- for me it became a refresher course and a boot camp.   <span id="freeText15902299040593104886" style="display:none">Everyone can be an entrepreneur. However, entrepreneurship is a tricky thing. Even those who have proper education may still struggle a little (or a lot) seeking for guidance how to get the ball rolling.<br /><br />"The Art of Startup Fundraising" by Alejandro Cremades is an informative read for aspiring entrepreneurs. Cremades presents a diverse approach in supporting start-up ideas – from the traditional methods we get from textbooks to street-smart tactics and to the utilization of new technological advancement. This book does not only tackle business financing but also stresses on the fundamentals of business. Pros and cons are weighed. Ins and outs are tackled. Comprehensive discussions from theories to applications are laid out.<br /><br />Sophisticated and highly informative. This book deserves attention and is highly recommended. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText10460527052604094321" style="display:none">"The Art of Startup Fundraising" by Alejandro Cremades is a necessary read for entrepreneurs and Venture Capital businesspersons. Fundraising is a critical phase in any business and Alejandro has tackled it professionally, including every minuscule point that a beginner needs to know. He has linked the entrepreneurs to the investor’s mind, suggesting them methods to improve fundraising process for startups. The author’s tone and language, which is a mixture of technical advice and everyday talk, makes it feasible for the reader to understand and benefit from the contents of this book. Instead of boring the reader with lengthy paragraphs, he has summed it up in bullets, thus, providing an easy learning for starters. His pragmatic approach and relevance are a great motivation for the reader, compelling him to follow the course as laid out by the book. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked

    }

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_11865558'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11865558-venture-deals?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Venture Deals<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/4395710.Brad_Feld?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Brad Feld<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.09 avg rating &mdash; 13,417 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2011\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer2894277220106324306\">Praise for Venture Deals\"My biggest nightmare is taking advantage of an entrepreneur without even realizing it. Brad and Jason are out to fix that problem with Venture D<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText2894277220106324306\" style=\"display:none\">Praise for Venture Deals&quot;My biggest nightmare is taking advantage of an entrepreneur without even realizing it. It happens because VCs are experts in financings and most entrepreneurs are not. Brad and Jason are out to fix that problem with Venture Deals. This book is long overdue and badly needed.&quot;Fred Wilson, Managing Partner, Union Square Ventures&quot;Feld and Mendelson pack a graduate-level course into this energetic and accessible book.?The authors\' frank style and incisive insight make this a must-read for high-growth company entrepreneurs, early-stage investors, and graduate students.?Start here if you want to understand venture capital deal structure and strategies.?I enthusiastically recommend.&quot;Brad Bernthal, CU Boulder, Associate Clinical Professor ofLaw, Technology Policy, Entrepreneurial Law&quot;A must-read book for entrepreneurs.?Brad and Jason demystify the overly complex world of term sheets and M&amp;A, cutting through the legalese and focusing on what really matters.?That\'s a good thing not just for entrepreneurs, but also for venture capitalists, angels, and lawyers.?Having an educated entrepreneur on the other side of the table means you spend your time negotiating the important issues and ultimately get to the right deal faster.&quot;Greg Gottesman, Managing Director, Madrona Venture Group&quot;Venture Deals is a must-read for any entrepreneur contemplating or currently leading a venture-backed company. Brad and Jason are highly respected investors who shoot straight from the hip and tell it like it is, bringing a level of transparency to a process that is rarely well understood. It\'s like having a venture capitalist as a best friend who is looking out for your best interests and happy to answer all of your questions.&quot;Emily Mendell, Vice President of Communications,National Venture Capital Association&quot;The adventure of starting and growing a company can be exhilarating or excruciatingor both. In 2016 in the United States alone, more than 31 percent of small business owners reported that they could not access adequate capital, and the lack of capital prevented them from growing the business/expanding operations, increasing inventory, or financing increased sales.Most business owners believe that their only feasible funding options are (1) savings or personal credit, (2) friends and family or (3) bank loans. They may have heard about venture capitalists or angel investors, but they don’t have enough information about what these investors do, what they can provide for a business, and on what terms. What’s worse, entrepreneurs often don’t know how to access the people who are looking to put their money into young companies with potential.Finally, business owners don’t have enough expertise to navigate the treacherous waters of outside funding. Many small companies don’t believe they are the type of company that gets funded. Even when business owners are brave enough to look for the right outside investors, they don’t know how to create the compelling pitches or how to structure the deals that will get them the funding to expand and grow.Crack the Funding Code will show readers how to find the money, create pitches that attract investors, and then structure fair, ethical deals that will bring them new sources of outside capital and invaluable professional advice. It will give readers the broader perspective—how funding works, how investors think, and what they need to hear to put their money where your mouth is. Every entrepreneur who reads this book will get easy-to-follow deal checklists, a roadmap of where and how to locate the best funding resources and top business mentors for their particular industry and/or geographical location, and a step-by-step process to create pitches that make their idea or business irresistible.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"11087287529804696468\" href=\"#\" People don\'t listen to advertisements, they listen to their peers. But why do people talk about certain products and ideas more than others? Why are some stories and rumors more infectious? And what makes online content go viral? Wharton marketing professor Jonah Berger has spent the last decade answering these questions. He\'s studied why New York Times articles make the paper\'s own Most E-mailed List, why products get word of mouth, and how social influence shapes everything from the cars we buy to the clothes we wear to the names we give our children. In this book, Berger reveals the secret science behind word-of-mouth and social transmission. Discover how six basic principles drive all sorts of things to become contagious, from consumer products and policy initiatives to workplace rumors and YouTube videos.Contagious combines groundbreaking research with powerful stories. Learn how a luxury steakhouse found popularity through the lowly cheese-steak, why anti-drug commercials might have actually increased drug use, and why more than 200 million consumers shared a video about one of the seemingly most boring products there is: a blender. If you\'ve wondered why certain stories get shared, e-mails get forwarded, or videos go viral, Contagious explains why, and shows how to leverage these concepts to craft contagious content. This book provides a set of specific, actionable techniques for helping information spread - for designing messages, advertisements, and information that people will share.               return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_53440290').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/14301938.Alejandro_Cremades">About Alejandro Cremades</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/14301938.Alejandro_Cremades"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1453029661p3/14301938.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer808602287292334976">Alejandro Cremades leads the vision and execution for Onevest as its Co-Founder and Executive Chairman. The Onevest ecosystem supports founders and investors in building successful ventures. Onevest provides technology products to connect founders, investors, advisors and influencers in the entrepreneurship community seamlessly and easily.<br/><br/>Onevest is currently operating 1000 Angels, which is the wo</span>
  <span id="freeText808602287292334976" style="display:none">Alejandro Cremades leads the vision and execution for Onevest as its Co-Founder and Executive Chairman. The Onevest ecosystem supports founders and investors in building successful ventures. Onevest provides technology products to connect founders, investors, advisors and influencers in the entrepreneurship community seamlessly and easily.<br /><br />Onevest is currently operating 1000 Angels, which is the world's largest digital-first, invitation-only investor network that allows members to build a venture portfolio free of management fees, carried interest, or large capital commitments. In addition, Onevest is operating CoFoundersLab, which is the leading matchmaking service for founders connecting them with other cofounders, advisors, and interns.<br /><br />Prior to Onevest, Alejandro was an attorney at King &amp; Spalding where he was involved in one of the largest investment arbitration cases in history with $113 billion at stake (Chevron vs. Ecuador).<br /><br />Alejandro guest lectures at NYU Stern School of Business and The Wharton Business School. Alejandro has been included in the Top 30 Under 30 lists of Vanity Fair, Entrepreneur Magazine, and GQ Magazine.<br /><br />Alejandro has also been involved with the JOBS Act since inception. He was invited to the White House and the US House of Representatives to provide his stands on the new regulatory changes.</span>
  <a data-text-id="808602287292334976" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
